name:X‚Äçi‚Äça‚Äçr‚Äçi‚Äçp‚Äça‚Äçn‚Äçd‚Äça

info:Stayed in April 2024

posted:Posted May 1, 2024
msg:Please give a big compliment to every staff member, especially the guys and girls at the front desk.
Location: If the itinerary includes Sanfang Qixiang, please give me your first choice of this hotel, and it is a deluxe Fangxiang room. It is directly connected to Fuzhou Station by subway. It takes only 5 minutes to walk from the subway station to the hotel. After leaving the hotel gate, you can walk ten steps (really only ten steps) to the Tower Lane of Sanfang Qixiang. If you want to buy something, you can turn around and enter Dongbai Shopping Mall. Huaxiang is across the road. It is so convenient. It is so pleasant to sit by the window and overlook the beautiful scenery of Sanfang Qixiang.
Service: As a person who has stayed in hotels for thousands of yuan and youth hostels for dozens of yuan, the service of this hotel is really commendable to me. First of all, you can swipe your card to get on the elevator. After reading the card, you will only reach the floor where you are staying, which gives you a full sense of security. All the staff you can see are in a very active working state, and they can keep a warm smile throughout the communication with customers. As a service industry worker, I know that this is not easy. The front desk staff will observe the needs of customers and provide services proactively. For example, my mother was not feeling well, and I ordered porridge for her. I sat in the lobby for less than 3 minutes while waiting for takeout on the first floor. A very gentle sister at the front desk took the initiative to bring me hot tea so that I could drink it while waiting. Later, one time, when I went out for a stroll, the porridge my mother ordered was delivered, and the front desk staff took the initiative to deliver it to the room. On the first day we arrived, the Didi driver canceled an order, which made us very angry. A handsome brother at the front desk called a taxi to Xichan Ancient Temple for us without saying a word, and the cleaning lady who cleaned the room price was also very polite, so that in the next few days of the trip, every time I stayed in a hotel, the aunt who traveled with me would compare this hotel with others.
Breakfast: The first thing I do when I wake up every day is to rush to the restaurant to see what special snacks are available today. The first day is peanut soup, the second day is taro paste, the third day is pot edge, and then I stayed for three days and ate Laohua for three days. I was so full that I went out for a walk every day. I was so happy~
Environment: The room is spacious and bright, and the hygiene is also very clean. It is very comfortable to live in. It is much better than the hotel in Xiamen that I stayed in later, which is known as the best~ Another advantage of living here is that if you get up early, you will get a quiet, deserted Sanfang Qixiang and the love tree, hahahaha.
To sum up: I like Fuzhou so much~ I haven‚Äôt played enough~ I will stay here for a few more days when I have time, and have a good time. I must stay in this hotel.
